	<!-- page embed js -->
    <script type="text/javascript">
        NEG.run(function (require) {
            var isProductList = 1;
            var productListBaseUrl = 'https://www.newegg.com/p/pl';
            var extraData = null;

            var jQuery = require("NEG.ThirdParty.jQuery");
            var qsb = require("NEG.Utility.QueryStringBuilder");
            var loading = require("Biz.Common.Loading2016");
            loading.hide();

            var nValueNotInNav = "8000";
            var initFilters = [];
            var changedGroups = {};
            var unSelections = {};
            var visibleButtons = {};
            var countKeys = function (obj) {
                var num = 0;
                for (var k in obj) {
                    if (obj.hasOwnProperty(k)) {
                        num += 1;
                    }
                }
                return num;
            };

            var urlArray = isProductList ? window.location.href.split("?") : productListBaseUrl.split("?");
            if (0) {
                urlArray = window.location.href.split("?");
                urlArray[0]=urlArray[0].substr(0, urlArray[0].lastIndexOf('Page-')-1);
            }
            var queryString = qsb(urlArray[1]);
            var nValue = queryString.get("N") && unescape(queryString.get("N")) != "-1" && unescape(queryString.get("N"));

            if (nValue) {
                jQuery.each(nValue.split(' '), function (index, value) {
                    if (initFilters.indexOf(value) < 0) {
                        initFilters.push(value);
                    }
                });

                if(JSON.parse("False".toLowerCase())){
                    initFilters = initFilters.filter(function(nValue){
                        return jQuery('input[neg-n-value="'+nValue+'"]').length>0 ||nValueNotInNav.indexOf(nValue)>=0;
                    });
                }
            } 

            var chkPriceRangeID = "#chbLeftNavPriceRange";
            var txtMinPriceID = "txtLeftNavPriceMin";
            var txtMaxPriceID = "txtLeftNavPriceMax";
            var chkLeftNavPriceRange = jQuery(chkPriceRangeID);
            var oriPriceChecked;
            var oriStrat;
            var oriEnd;
            var priceRangeGroupId;
            if (chkLeftNavPriceRange.length > 0) {
                oriPriceChecked = chkLeftNavPriceRange.prop("checked");
                oriStrat = jQuery("#" + txtMinPriceID).val();
                oriEnd = jQuery("#" + txtMaxPriceID).val();
                priceRangeGroupId = chkLeftNavPriceRange.attr("name");
            }

            var handler = function () {

                loading.hide();
                loading.show();

                for (var gid in visibleButtons) {
                    if (!visibleButtons.hasOwnProperty(gid)) {
                        continue;
                    }
                    var btn = visibleButtons[gid];
                    btn.html('<i class="fa fa-refresh fa-spin"></i>' + btn.text());
                }
                var allNValues = [];
                initFilters.forEach(function (initN) {
                    if (!unSelections.hasOwnProperty(initN)) {
                        allNValues.push(initN);
                    }
                });

                for (var gid in changedGroups) {

                    if (!changedGroups.hasOwnProperty(gid)) {
                        continue;
                    }
                    var group = changedGroups[gid];
                    for (var changeN in group) {
                        if (!group.hasOwnProperty(changeN)) {
                            continue;
                        }

                        if (group[changeN].checked) {
                            group[changeN].values.forEach(function (val) {
                                if (allNValues.indexOf(val) < 0 && !unSelections.hasOwnProperty(val)) {
                                    allNValues.push(val);
                                }
                            });
                            if (allNValues.indexOf(changeN) < 0 && !unSelections.hasOwnProperty(changeN)) {
                                allNValues.push(changeN);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (chkLeftNavPriceRange.length > 0 && chkLeftNavPriceRange.prop("checked")) {
                    var priceRangeOriNvalue = chkLeftNavPriceRange.attr('neg-n-value');
                    if (priceRangeOriNvalue) {
                        jQuery.each(priceRangeOriNvalue.split(' '), function (index, value) {
                            if (allNValues.indexOf(value) < 0 && !unSelections.hasOwnProperty(value)) {
                                allNValues.push(value);
                            }
                        });
                    }
                }

                var newNValue = "-1";
                if (allNValues.length > 0) {
                    newNValue = allNValues.join(' ');
                }
                queryString.set("N", newNValue);

                var priceRangeStr = "LeftPriceRange";
                if (chkLeftNavPriceRange.length > 0) {
                    if (chkLeftNavPriceRange.prop("checked")) {

                        if (jQuery("#" + txtMinPriceID).val() == "") {
                            jQuery("#" + txtMinPriceID).val("0");
                        }

                        var minVal = jQuery("#" + txtMinPriceID).val().replace(/,/g, "");
                        var maxVal = jQuery('#' + txtMaxPriceID).val().replace(/,/g, "");

                        var priceRangeValue = "0";

                        if (minVal.length > 0) {
                            priceRangeValue = minVal;
                        }

                        if (maxVal.length > 0) {
                            priceRangeValue += " " + maxVal;
                        }

                        queryString.set(priceRangeStr, priceRangeValue);
                    } else {
                        if (queryString.get(priceRangeStr)) {
                            queryString.remove(priceRangeStr);
                        }
                    }
                }

                if (extraData) {
                    for (var i = 0, length = extraData.length; i < length; i++) {
                        queryString.set(extraData[i].key, extraData[i].value);
                    }
                }
                if (queryString.get("page")) {
                    queryString.remove("page");
                }
                if (!!window.ActiveXObject || "ActiveXObject" in window) {
                    jQuery(".left-nav input[type='checkBox']:checked").prop('checked', false);
                    jQuery(".left-nav input[orignal='checked']").prop('checked', true);

                    jQuery("#txtLeftNavPriceMin").attr('value', oriStrat);
                    jQuery("#txtLeftNavPriceMax").attr('value', oriEnd);
                }
                setTimeout(function () {
                    window.location.href = urlArray[0] + "?" + queryString.toString(true);
                }, 200);
            };

            var updateGroup = function (groupId, n, newStatus, values) {
                if ((initFilters.indexOf(n) >= 0 && newStatus) || (initFilters.indexOf(n) < 0 && !newStatus)) {
                    if (changedGroups.hasOwnProperty(groupId)) {
                        delete changedGroups[groupId][n];
                        if (countKeys(changedGroups[groupId]) === 0) {
                            delete changedGroups[groupId];
                        }
                    }
                } else {
                    if (!changedGroups.hasOwnProperty(groupId)) {
                        changedGroups[groupId] = {};
                    }
                    changedGroups[groupId][n] = { checked: newStatus, values: values.split(' ') };
                }
                if (newStatus) {
                    delete unSelections[n];
                } else {
                    unSelections[n] = '';
                }
            };

            jQuery("#" + txtMinPriceID + ",#" + txtMaxPriceID).focus(function () {
                chkLeftNavPriceRange.attr("checked", "checked");
                if (visibleButtons.hasOwnProperty(priceRangeGroupId)) {
                    return;
                }
                showApplyButton(priceRangeGroupId);
            });

            jQuery("#" + txtMinPriceID + ",#" + txtMaxPriceID).change(function () {
                jQuery(this).val(jQuery(this).val().replace(/[^0-9.]/g, ''));

                if (jQuery(this).val().substr(0, 1) == ".") {
                    jQuery(this).val("0" + jQuery(this).val());
                }

                var oriTxtValue = jQuery(this).val();
                var num = parseFloat(oriTxtValue);
                if (!isNaN(num)) {

                    var numStr = num + "";
                    var indexdot = numStr.indexOf(".");
                    if (indexdot != -1) {
                        numStr = numStr.substr(0, indexdot + 3);
                    }

                    var formatValue = numStr.replace(/\d{1,3}(?=(\d{3})+(\.\d*)?$)/g, '$&,');
                    var dotindex = formatValue.indexOf(".");
                    if (dotindex == -1) {
                        if (endWith(oriTxtValue, ".0")) {
                            formatValue += ".0";
                        } else if (endWith(oriTxtValue, ".00") || endWithZero(oriTxtValue)) {
                            formatValue += ".00";
                        }
                    } else {
                        if (endWith(oriTxtValue, "0")) {
                            if (dotindex + 2 == formatValue.length) {
                                formatValue += "0";
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    jQuery(this).val(formatValue);
                } else {
                    jQuery(this).val("");
                }
            });

            var endWith = function (oriStr, endStr) {
                var d = oriStr.length - endStr.length;
                return (d >= 0 && oriStr.lastIndexOf(endStr) == d);
            };

            var endWithZero = function (oriStr) {
                var dotindex = oriStr.lastIndexOf(".");

                if (dotindex > -1 && dotindex + 1 < oriStr.length) {
                    var isAllZero = true;
                    for (var i = dotindex + 1; i < oriStr.length; i++) {
                        if (oriStr[i] != "0") {
                            isAllZero = false;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                    return isAllZero;
                } else {
                    return false;
                }
            };

            var applyChange = function (groupId, n, newStatus, values) {
                updateGroup(groupId, n, newStatus, values);
                if (changedGroups.hasOwnProperty(groupId)) {
                    if (!visibleButtons.hasOwnProperty(groupId)) {
                        showApplyButton(groupId);
                    }
                } else if (visibleButtons.hasOwnProperty(groupId)) {

                    if (priceRangeGroupId == groupId) {
                        var currentPriceChecked = chkLeftNavPriceRange.prop("checked");
                        var currentStrat = jQuery("#" + txtMinPriceID).val();
                        var currentEnd = jQuery('#' + txtMaxPriceID).val();
                        if ((oriPriceChecked == false && currentPriceChecked == false) ||
                        (oriPriceChecked == currentPriceChecked && currentEnd == oriEnd && currentStrat == oriStrat)) {
                            hideApplyButton(groupId);
                        }
                    } else {
                        hideApplyButton(groupId);
                    }
                }
            };

            var priceRangeClick = function (groupId) {
                var currentPriceChecked = chkLeftNavPriceRange.prop("checked");
                if (oriPriceChecked != currentPriceChecked) {
                    if (visibleButtons.hasOwnProperty(groupId)) {
                        return;
                    }

                    showApplyButton(groupId);
                } else if (oriPriceChecked == currentPriceChecked) {
                    if (visibleButtons.hasOwnProperty(groupId)) {
                        if (!changedGroups.hasOwnProperty(groupId)) {
                            if (oriPriceChecked == false) {
                                hideApplyButton(groupId);
                                return;
                            }

                            var currentStrat = jQuery("#" + txtMinPriceID).val();
                            var currentEnd = jQuery("#" + txtMaxPriceID).val();
                            if (currentEnd == oriEnd && currentStrat == oriStrat) {
                                hideApplyButton(groupId);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            };

            var hideApplyButton = function (groupId) {
                visibleButtons[groupId].css("display", "none");
                visibleButtons[groupId].unbind('click');
                delete visibleButtons[groupId];
            };

            var showApplyButton = function (groupId) {
                var applyBtn = jQuery('#fab_' + groupId);
                applyBtn.css("display", "block");
                applyBtn.click(function () {
                    handler();
                });
                visibleButtons[groupId] = applyBtn;
            };

            var isAllChildrenChecked = function ($container) {
                return $container.find(".form-checkbox input[type='checkbox']").length === $container.find(".form-checkbox input[type='checkbox']:checked").length;
            };

            var hasAnyChildChecked = function ($container) {
                return $container.find(".form-checkbox input[type='checkbox']:checked").length > 0;
            };

            var container = jQuery(".left-nav")[0];
            NEG(container).on("click", function (e) {

                var target = e.target || e.srcElement;
                var targetId = target && target.id;
                var targetType = target && target.type;

                if (targetType != "checkbox" || (!targetId)) {
                    return;
                }

                var $filter = jQuery(target);
                var groupId = $filter.attr('name');

                if (targetId == "chbLeftNavPriceRange") {
                    priceRangeClick(groupId);
                    return;
                }

                var values = $filter.attr('neg-n-value');
                var isParentNode = $filter.attr('neg-n-parent');
                if (isParentNode) {

                    var $children = $filter.parents('div.filter-box-label').next('ul.filter-box-list');
                    $children.find("li div label input[type='checkbox']").prop("checked", !!target.checked);
                    $children.find("li div label input[type='checkbox']").each(function () {
                        applyChange(groupId, this.id, false, jQuery(this).attr('neg-n-value'));
                    });
                    applyChange(groupId, targetId, !!target.checked, values);
                } else {
                    var $childNode = $filter.parents("li ul.filter-box-list");
                    if ($childNode.length > 0) {
                        var $parentNode = $childNode.prev("div.filter-box-label");
                        var $parentTarget = $parentNode.find("input[type='checkbox']");
                        var parentId = $parentTarget.attr("id");
                        var parentValues = $parentTarget.attr("neg-n-value");
                        var allChildrenChecked = isAllChildrenChecked($childNode);
                        var anyChecked = hasAnyChildChecked($childNode);
                        $parentTarget.prop("checked", allChildrenChecked);
                        $parentTarget.prop("indeterminate", !allChildrenChecked && anyChecked);

                        if (allChildrenChecked) {
                            applyChange(groupId, parentId, true, parentValues);
                            $childNode.find(".form-checkbox input[type='checkbox']").each(function () {
                                applyChange(groupId, this.id, false, jQuery(this).attr('neg-n-value'));
                            });
                        } else {
                            applyChange(groupId, parentId, false, parentValues);
                            $childNode.find(".form-checkbox input[type='checkbox']").each(function () {
                                applyChange(groupId, this.id, jQuery(this).prop('checked'), jQuery(this).attr('neg-n-value'));
                            });
                        }
                    } else {
                        applyChange(groupId, targetId, !!target.checked, values);
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    NEG.domReady(function () {
        var cfg = Biz.Product.CompareConfig2019;
        NEG.run(function (require) {
            var bizCompareModule = require("Biz.Product.Compare2019");
            var $ = require("NEG.ThirdParty.JQuery");
            var options = {
                enableCompare2019: true,
                maxSubCategoryGroup: 3,
                enableRecommendation: true,
                maxRecommendItems:10,
                goCompare: function () {
                    document.getElementById('CurrentUrl2019') && (document.getElementById('CurrentUrl2019').value = window.location);
                    var compareData = this.getCompareData2019FirstSubCateIdsAndItemNumbers();
                    var compareString = this.getCompareListString2019(compareData);
                
                    var items = compareData.itemList;
                    var itempers = [];

                    cfg.baseQueryString.set("CompareItemList", compareString);
                   
                    var citem = "";
                    var percm = "";
                    for (var mi = 0; mi < items.length; mi++) {
                        citem = items[mi];
                        if (citem != null && citem.length > 0) {
                            if (itempers[citem] != null && itempers[citem].length > 0) {
                                percm = percm + ';' + citem + ':' + itempers[citem];
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    if (percm.length > 0) {
                        percm = percm.substring(1, percm.length);
                    }
                    if (percm.length > 0) {
                        cfg.baseQueryString.set("percm", encodeURIComponent(percm));
                    }

                    var qs = cfg.baseQueryString.toString();
                    document.forms.compareform2019.action = cfg.PageUrlAlias.compare + "?" + qs;
                    document.forms.compareform2019.submit();
                }
            };

            var bizCompare = bizCompareModule(options);

            

        });
    });
</script>

<span id="checkbox_compare" class="hid-text">Add To Compare</span>
